[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed or edge-case inputs.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The buffer allocation and bounds checks around line [0m[1;36m634[0m[39m of [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/shadowsocks/src/json.c` in `json_parse_ex`.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The higher-level `json_parse` logic in the same file [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m958[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvokes `json_parse_ex`.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The overall memory management strategy of the JSON parser—particularly how it [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgrows or reads buffers when parsing complex structures.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The interaction between the fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`src/json_fuzz.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the parser [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry point to understand which inputs trigger the overflow.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis information should guide a focused code review of the JSON parsing logic to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand how and why the out-of-bounds read occurs under fuzzing conditions.[0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer run on the shadowsocks JSON parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`src/json.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggered an [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer heap‐buffer‐overflow in `json_parse_ex` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m634[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The user [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempted a patch to add explicit handling for the JSON literals `null`, `true`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `false`—replacing and extending the existing switch‐case logic. When this patch[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwas applied, the code failed to compile with numerous errors: undeclared [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`json_true`, `json_false`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, duplicate `case` labels for `[0m[32m't'[0m[39m` and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[32m'f'[0m[39m`, missing labels [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`e_unknown_value`, `e_alloc_failure`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, syntax mismatches [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39munmatched braces, stray `else`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and spurious lines deep in the file.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **What happened**: During fuzzing, the parser reads one byte past a heap [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while interpreting input in `json_parse_ex`. ASan reports a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read overflow at `json.[0m[1;92mc:634:55[0m[39m`.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Fuzzer context**: LLVMFuzzer calls into `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` → [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_parse`. The input was a single test case run repeatedly.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Key log entries**:  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • “READ of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m … [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte region”  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Stack trace roots in `json_parse_ex` → `json_parse` → [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Shows that the overflow occurs during the character‐by‐character parsing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloop.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Goal**: Consolidate and correct literal parsing for `null`, plus add [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicit branches for `true` and `false`, instead of letting the default/fallback [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnumeric‐or‐error logic handle them.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Patch location**: Around line [0m[1;36m628[0m[39m in `src/json.c`, inside the big `switch [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` that dispatches based on the current character.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Key changes**:  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Replaced an existing block labeled `case [0m[32m'n'[0m[39m:` and merged numeric default [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Added new `case [0m[32m't'[0m[39m: … json_true` and `case [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m: … json_false` blocks.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Adjusted pointer‐advancement checks from “< [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m” to “< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m” [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand “< [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m” for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`false`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, incrementing `state.ptr` appropriately.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Intended to `goto` shared error labels ­— `e_unknown_value`, [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`e_alloc_failure`.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Compilation Result  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Applying the patch produced a cascade of compiler errors:  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Undeclared identifiers**: `json_true`, `json_false` are not defined anywhere[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the codebase.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Duplicate case labels**: The file already contained `case [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m:` and `case [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m't'[0m[39m:` blocks before the patch, so new ones collide.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Missing labels**: Labels such as `e_unknown_value`, `e_alloc_failure`, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`e_failed`, `e_overflow` are not in scope at the insertion point.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Syntax errors**:  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Unmatched or extraneous braces.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Stray `else` statements with no matching `if`.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Unexpected lines [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`alloc = root;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and broken function epilogue [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`return [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Header mismatches**: The patch refers to functions and types not declared in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json.h`.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Switch‐case in `json_parse_ex`**: Review the existing structure of the big [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`switch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` covering `[0m[32m'n'[0m[39m`, `[0m[32m't'[0m[39m`, `[0m[32m'f'[0m[39m`, numbers, strings, etc. Determine how [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meach literal is handled, and why buffer boundaries aren’t checked properly.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Definitions of JSON value types**: In `json.h`, inspect how `json_null`, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_integer`, and other enum constants or function pointers are declared. Verify [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhether `json_true`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`json_false` exist or should be named differently [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_boolean`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Error‐handling labels**: Locate the declarations of `e_alloc_failure`, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`e_unknown_value`, etc., and see how control flows to them. Ensure any patch reuses[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe exact labels.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Buffer‐bound checks**: Trace how `state.ptr`, `state.first_pass`, and `end` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare defined and used. The root overflow likely stems from insufficient checks when [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madvancing `state.ptr` past `end`.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Numeric parsing branch**: Since the original default case handled digits and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msigns, inspect that entire path for similar out‐of‐bounds reads.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
